 `json:\"lookback_from\"` // Start of measurement period\n40\t\tModels              []string      `json:\"models\"`\n41\t\tModelUsages         []ModelUsage  `json:\"model_usages\"` // Per-model breakdown\n42\t\tAvailable           bool          `json:\"available\"`\n43\t\tError               string        `json:\"error,omitempty\"`\n44\t\tLastUpdate          time.Time     `json:\"last_update\"`\n45\t}\n46\t\n47\t// TokenCollector collects and aggregates token usage from Claude Code sessions\n48\ttype TokenCollector struct {\n49\t\tprojectsDirs  []string  // Root directories to scan for JSONL files\n50\t\tlookbackFrom  time.Time // Only include data from this time onwards\n51\t\tcache         *TokenCache\n52\t\tstopIngestion chan struct{} // Closed to stop the background ingestion goroutine\n53\t}\n54\t\n55\t// GetMondayNineAM returns the most recent Monday at 9am local time\n56\t// If today is Monday before 9am, returns last Monday's 9am\n57\tfunc GetMondayNineAM() time.Time {\n58\t\tnow := time.Now()\n59\t\t// Find the most recent Monday\n60\t\tweekday := int(now.Weekday())\n61\t\tif weekday == 0 {\n62\t\t\tweekday = 7 // Sunday becomes 7 for easier math\n63\t\t}\n64\t\tdaysUntilMonday := weekday - 1 // Days since Monday (Mon=0, Tue=1, ...)\n65\t\n66\t\t// Start of Monday (midnight)\n67\t\tmonday := now.AddDate(0, 0, -daysUntilMonday)\n68\t\tmonday = time.Date(monday.Year(), monday.Month(), monday.Day(), 9, 0, 0, 0, monday.Location())\n69\t\n70\t\t// If we haven't reached 9am on Monday yet, go back to previous Monday\n71\t\tif monday.After(now) {\n72\t\t\tmonday = monday.AddDate(0, 0, -7)\n73\t\t}\n74\t\n75\t\treturn monday\n76\t}\n77\t\n78\t// buildDefaultProjectsDirs returns the list of root directories to scan.\n79\t// Always includes ~/.claude/projects as the primary directory.\n80\t// Also reads CCDASH_EXTRA_DIRS (colon-separated) for additional roots.\n81\tfunc buildDefaultProjectsDirs(home string) []string {\n82\t\tvar dirs []string\n83\t\tif home != \"\" {\n84\t\t\tdirs = append(dirs, filepath.Join(home, \".claude\", \"projects\"))\n85\t\t}\n86\t\tif extra := os.Getenv(\"CCDASH_EXTRA_DIRS\"); extra != \"\" {\n87\t\t\tfor _, d := range strings.Split(extra, \":\") {\n88\t\t\t\tif d = strings.TrimSpace(d); d != \"\" {\n89\t\t\t\t\tdirs = append(dirs, d)\n90\t\t\t\t}\n91\t\t\t}\n92\t\t}\n93\t\treturn dirs\n94\t}\n95\t\n96\t// NewTokenCollector creates a new TokenCollector with default Monday 9am lookback\n97\tfunc NewTokenCollector() *TokenCollector {\n98\t\thome, _ := os.UserHomeDir()\n99\t\ttc := &TokenCollector{\n100\t\t\tprojectsDirs: buildDefaultProjectsDirs(home),\n101\t\t\tlookbackFrom: GetMondayNineAM(),\n102\t\t\tcache:        NewTokenCache(),\n103\t\t}\n104\t\ttc.startBackgroundIngestion()\n105\t\treturn tc\n106\t}\n107\t\n108\t// NewTokenCollectorWithLookback creates a TokenCollector with a custom lookback time\n109\tfunc NewTokenCollectorWithLookback(lookbackFrom time.Time) *TokenCollector {\n110\t\thome, _ := os.UserHomeDir()\n111\t\ttc := &TokenCollector{\n112\t\t\tprojectsDirs: buildDefaultProjectsDirs(home),\n113\t\t\tlookbackFrom: lookbackFrom,\n114\t\t\tcache:        NewTokenCache(),\n115\t\t}\n116\t\ttc.startBackgroundIngestion()\n117\t\treturn tc\n118\t}\n119\t\n120\t// NewTokenCollectorWithPath creates a TokenCollector with a custom path (for testing)\n121\tfunc NewTokenCollectorWithPath(path string) *TokenCollector {\n122\t\ttc := &TokenCollector{\n123\t\t\tprojectsDirs: []string{path},\n124\t\t\tlookbackFrom: GetMondayNineAM(),\n125\t\t\tcache:        NewTokenCache(),\n126\t\t}\n127\t\ttc.startBackgroundIngestion()\n128\t\treturn tc\n129\t}\n130\t\n131\t// startBackgroundIngestion starts a goroutine that ingests JSONL files into SQLite\n132\t// independently of the UI refresh cycle. This decouples slow file I/O from the\n133\t// fast DB query that populates the token panel.\n134\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) startBackgroundIngestion() {\n135\t\ttc.stopIngestion = make(chan struct{})\n136\t\tgo func() {\n137\t\t\t// Run immediately so data is available as soon as possible\n138\t\t\ttc.runIngestionCycle()\n139\t\n140\t\t\tticker := time.NewTicker(30 * time.Second)\n141\t\t\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n142\t\t\tfor {\n143\t\t\t\tselect {\n144\t\t\t\tcase <-tc.stopIngestion:\n145\t\t\t\t\treturn\n146\t\t\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n147\t\t\t\t\ttc.runIngestionCycle()\n148\t\t\t\t}\n149\t\t\t}\n150\t\t}()\n151\t}\n152\t\n153\t// StopBackgroundIngestion shuts down the background ingestion goroutine.\n154\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) StopBackgroundIngestion() {\n155\t\tif tc.stopIngestion != nil {\n156\t\t\tclose(tc.stopIngestion)\n157\t\t\ttc.stopIngestion = nil\n158\t\t}\n159\t}\n160\t\n161\t// runIngestionCycle scans all JSONL files and ingests new data into SQLite.\n162\t// Called by the background goroutine; uses ingestMu so it never blocks fast\n163\t// cache/lease operations.\n164\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) runIngestionCycle() {\n165\t\tif len(tc.projectsDirs) == 0 {\n166\t\t\treturn\n167\t\t}\n168\t\tprojectDirs, err := tc.findAllProjectDirs()\n169\t\tif err != nil || len(projectDirs) == 0 {\n170\t\t\treturn\n171\t\t}\n172\t\n173\t\tvar files []string\n174\t\tfor _, projectDir := range projectDirs {\n175\t\t\tdirFiles, err := findJSONLFilesRecursive(projectDir)\n176\t\t\tif err != nil {\n177\t\t\t\tcontinue\n178\t\t\t}\n179\t\t\tfiles = append(files, dirFiles...)\n180\t\t}\n181\t\n182\t\tcompleteThreshold := GetFileCompleteThreshold()\n183\t\tfor _, file := range files {\n184\t\t\tfileInfo, err := os.Stat(file)\n185\t\t\tif err != nil {\n186\t\t\t\tcontinue\n187\t\t\t}\n188\t\n189\t\t\tif agg, ok := tc.cache.GetFileAggregate(file); ok && agg.IsComplete {\n190\t\t\t\tif !fileInfo.ModTime().After(agg.CompletedAt) {\n191\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n192\t\t\t\t}\n193\t\t\t\ttc.cache.MarkFileActive(file)\n194\t\t\t}\n195\t\n196\t\t\tif time.Since(fileInfo.ModTime()) > completeThreshold {\n197\t\t\t\tif err := tc.ingestJSONLFile(file); err == nil {\n198\t\t\t\t\ttc.cache.MarkFileComplete(file)\n199\t\t\t\t}\n200\t\t\t\tcontinue\n201\t\t\t}\n202\t\n203\t\t\ttc.ingestJSONLFile(file)\n204\t\t}\n205\t}\n206\t\n207\t// AddProjectsDir adds an additional root directory to scan for JSONL files.\n208\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) AddProjectsDir(path string) {\n209\t\ttc.projectsDirs = append(tc.projectsDirs, path)\n210\t}\n211\t\n212\t// SetLookback sets the lookback time filter\n213\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) SetLookback(t time.Time) {\n214\t\ttc.lookbackFrom = t\n215\t}\n216\t\n217\t// GetLookback returns the current lookback time\n218\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) GetLookback() time.Time {\n219\t\treturn tc.lookbackFrom\n220\t}\n221\t\n222\t// GetCache returns the underlying token cache for shared metrics operations\n223\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) GetCache() *TokenCache {\n224\t\treturn tc.cache\n225\t}\n226\t\n227\t// claudeMessage represents the structure of Claude API messages in JSONL\n228\ttype claudeMessage struct {\n229\t\tMessage   messageData `json:\"message\"`\n230\t\tTimestamp string      `json:\"timestamp\"`\n231\t\tType      string      `json:\"type\"`\n232\t}\n233\t\n234\t// messageData contains the actual API response\n235\ttype messageData struct {\n236\t\tModel string    `json:\"model\"`\n237\t\tUsage usageData `json:\"usage\"`\n238\t}\n239\t\n240\t// usageData contains token usage information\n241\ttype usageData struct {\n242\t\tInputTokens              int64         `json:\"input_tokens\"`\n243\t\tCacheCreationInputTokens int64         `json:\"cache_creation_input_tokens\"`\n244\t\tCacheReadInputTokens     int64         `json:\"cache_read_input_tokens\"`\n245\t\tOutputTokens             int64         `json:\"output_tokens\"`\n246\t\tCacheCreation            cacheCreation `json:\"cache_creation\"`\n247\t}\n248\t\n249\t// cacheCreation contains detailed cache creation token breakdown\n250\ttype cacheCreation struct {\n251\t\tEphemeral5mInputTokens int64 `json:\"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens\"`\n252\t\tEphemeral1hInputTokens int64 `json:\"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens\"`\n253\t}\n254\t\n255\t// Collect returns token metrics from the SQLite cache. File ingestion runs in a\n256\t// background goroutine (started by the constructor) so this method only executes\n257\t// the fast DB query and never blocks on file I/O.\n258\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) Collect() (*TokenMetrics, error) {\n259\t\tmetrics := &TokenMetrics{\n260\t\t\tAvailable:    false,\n261\t\t\tLastUpdate:   time.Now(),\n262\t\t\tLookbackFrom: tc.lookbackFrom,\n263\t\t\tModels:       []string{},\n264\t\t}\n265\t\n266\t\tif len(tc.projectsDirs) == 0 {\n267\t\t\tmetrics.Error = \"No projects directories configured\"\n268\t\t\treturn metrics, nil\n269\t\t}\n270\t\n271\t\t// Query SQLite using hybrid approach (pre-aggregated + active events)\n272\t\taggregated, err := tc.cache.QueryTokensHybrid(tc.lookbackFrom)\n273\t\tif err != nil {\n274\t\t\tmetrics.Error = fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to query token cache: %v\", err)\n275\t\t\treturn metrics, nil\n276\t\t}\n277\t\n278\t\t// Populate metrics from query results\n279\t\tmetrics.InputTokens = aggregated.InputTokens\n280\t\tmetrics.OutputTokens = aggregated.OutputTokens\n281\t\tmetrics.CacheReadTokens = aggregated.CacheReadTokens\n282\t\tmetrics.CacheCreationTokens = aggregated.CacheCreationTokens\n283\t\tmetrics.TotalTokens = aggregated.InputTokens + aggregated.OutputTokens +\n284\t\t\taggregated.CacheReadTokens + aggregated.CacheCreationTokens\n285\t\tmetrics.Prompts = aggregated.EventCount\n286\t\tmetrics.EarliestTimestamp = aggregated.EarliestTimestamp\n287\t\tmetrics.LatestTimestamp = aggregated.LatestTimestamp\n288\t\n289\t\tif !aggregated.EarliestTimestamp.IsZero() && !aggregated.LatestTimestamp.IsZero() {\n290\t\t\tmetrics.TimeSpan = aggregated.LatestTimestamp.Sub(aggregated.EarliestTimestamp)\n291\t\t}\n292\t\n293\t\t// Build model list and per-model usage\n294\t\tvar totalCost float64\n295\t\tmetrics.ModelUsages = make([]ModelUsage, 0, len(aggregated.ModelMetrics))\n296\t\n297\t\tfor model, mm := range aggregated.ModelMetrics {\n298\t\t\tmetrics.Models = append(metrics.Models, model)\n299\t\n300\t\t\tpricing := getPricingForModel(model)\n301\t\t\tinputCost := float64(mm.InputTokens) * pricing.InputPerMillion / 1_000_000\n302\t\t\toutputCost := float64(mm.OutputTokens) * pricing.OutputPerMillion / 1_000_000\n303\t\t\tcacheReadCost := float64(mm.CacheReadTokens) * pricing.CacheReadPerMillion / 1_000_000\n304\t\t\tcacheCreateCost := float64(mm.CacheCreationTokens) * pricing.CacheCreatePerMillion / 1_000_000\n305\t\t\tmodelCost := inputCost + outputCost + cacheReadCost + cacheCreateCost\n306\t\n307\t\t\tusage := ModelUsage{\n308\t\t\t\tModel:               model,\n309\t\t\t\tInputTokens:         mm.InputTokens,\n310\t\t\t\tOutputTokens:        mm.OutputTokens,\n311\t\t\t\tCacheReadTokens:     mm.CacheReadTokens,\n312\t\t\t\tCacheCreationTokens: mm.CacheCreationTokens,\n313\t\t\t\tTotalTokens:         mm.InputTokens + mm.OutputTokens + mm.CacheReadTokens + mm.CacheCreationTokens,\n314\t\t\t\tCost:                modelCost,\n315\t\t\t}\n316\t\t\tmetrics.ModelUsages = append(metrics.ModelUsages, usage)\n317\t\t\ttotalCost += modelCost\n318\t\t}\n319\t\n320\t\tsort.Strings(metrics.Models)\n321\t\n322\t\t// Sort model usages by cost (highest first)\n323\t\tsort.Slice(metrics.ModelUsages, func(i, j int) bool {\n324\t\t\treturn metrics.ModelUsages[i].Cost > metrics.ModelUsages[j].Cost\n325\t\t})\n326\t\n327\t\tmetrics.TotalCost = totalCost\n328\t\n329\t\t// Calculate session average rate\n330\t\tif metrics.TimeSpan > 0 {\n331\t\t\tminutes := metrics.TimeSpan.Minutes()\n332\t\t\tif minutes > 0 {\n333\t\t\t\tmetrics.SessionAvgRate = float64(metrics.TotalTokens) / minutes\n334\t\t\t}\n335\t\t}\n336\t\n337\t\t// Calculate 60-second window rate from recent events\n338\t\trecentEvents, err := tc.cache.QueryRecentEvents(60)\n339\t\tif err == nil && len(recentEvents) > 0 {\n340\t\t\tmetrics.Rate = tc.calculate60sRate(recentEvents)\n341\t\t}\n342\t\n343\t\tmetrics.Available = true\n344\t\treturn metrics, nil\n345\t}\n346\t\n347\t// ingestJSONLFile reads a JSONL file and inserts new events into SQLite\n348\t// Returns an error if database operations fail (for proper error handling)\n349\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) ingestJSONLFile(filename string) error {\n350\t\tif tc.cache == nil {\n351\t\t\treturn nil\n352\t\t}\n353\t\n354\t\t// Check file modification time\n355\t\tfileInfo, err := os.Stat(filename)\n356\t\tif err != nil {\n357\t\t\treturn nil // File may have been deleted, not a critical error\n358\t\t}\n359\t\n360\t\t// Get last processed state\n361\t\tlastLine, lastMod, exists := tc.cache.GetFileState(filename)\n362\t\n363\t\t// If file hasn't been modified since last processing, skip\n364\t\tif exists && !fileInfo.ModTime().After(lastMod) {\n365\t\t\treturn nil\n366\t\t}\n367\t\n368\t\t// If file was modified (truncated/rewritten), invalidate and reprocess\n369\t\tif exists && fileInfo.ModTime().After(lastMod) {\n370\t\t\t// Check if file was truncated (new size < last line count implies rewrite)\n371\t\t\t// For safety, we'll just process from where we left off\n372\t\t\t// but if file was completely rewritten, invalidate\n373\t\t\tfile, err := os.Open(filename)\n374\t\t\tif err != nil {\n375\t\t\t\treturn nil // File may have been deleted\n376\t\t\t}\n377\t\t\tdefer file.Close()\n378\t\n379\t\t\t// Count current lines\n380\t\t\tvar currentLineCount int64\n381\t\t\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(file)\n382\t\t\tbuf := make([]byte, 0, 1024*1024)\n383\t\t\tscanner.Buffer(buf, 10*1024*1024)\n384\t\t\tfor scanner.Scan() {\n385\t\t\t\tcurrentLineCount++\n386\t\t\t}\n387\t\n388\t\t\t// If file has fewer lines than we processed, it was rewritten\n389\t\t\tif currentLineCount < lastLine {\n390\t\t\t\tif err := tc.cache.InvalidateFile(filename); err != nil {\n391\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to invalidate file %s: %w\", filename, err)\n392\t\t\t\t}\n393\t\t\t\tlastLine = 0\n394\t\t\t}\n395\t\t}\n396\t\n397\t\t// Open file for processing\n398\t\tfile, err := os.Open(filename)\n399\t\tif err != nil {\n400\t\t\treturn nil // File may have been deleted\n401\t\t}\n402\t\tdefer file.Close()\n403\t\n404\t\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(file)\n405\t\tbuf := make([]byte, 0, 1024*1024)\n406\t\tscanner.Buffer(buf, 10*1024*1024)\n407\t\n408\t\tvar lineNumber int64\n409\t\tvar events []TokenEvent\n410\t\n411\t\tfor scanner.Scan() {\n412\t\t\tlineNumber++\n413\t\n414\t\t\t// Skip already processed lines\n415\t\t\tif lineNumber <= lastLine {\n416\t\t\t\tcontinue\n417\t\t\t}\n418\t\n419\t\t\tvar msg claudeMessage\n420\t\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(scanner.Bytes(), &msg); err != nil {\n421\t\t\t\tcontinue\n422\t\t\t}\n423\t\n424\t\t\t// Only process assistant messages (count all requests, even with zero tokens)\n425\t\t\tif msg.Type != \"assistant\" {\n426\t\t\t\tcontinue\n427\t\t\t}\n428\t\n429\t\t\t// Parse timestamp\n430\t\t\ttimestamp, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339Nano, msg.Timestamp)\n431\t\t\tif err != nil {\n432\t\t\t\tcontinue\n433\t\t\t}\n434\t\n435\t\t\tusage := msg.Message.Usage\n436\t\t\tcacheCreation := usage.CacheCreationInputTokens\n437\t\t\tif cacheCreation == 0 {\n438\t\t\t\tcacheCreation = usage.CacheCreation.Ephemeral5mInputTokens +\n439\t\t\t\t\tusage.CacheCreation.Ephemeral1hInputTokens\n440\t\t\t}\n441\t\n442\t\t\tevents = append(events, TokenEvent{\n443\t\t\t\tTimestamp:           timestamp,\n444\t\t\t\tModel:               msg.Message.Model,\n445\t\t\t\tInputTokens:         usage.InputTokens,\n446\t\t\t\tOutputTokens:        usage.OutputTokens,\n447\t\t\t\tCacheReadTokens:     usage.CacheReadInputTokens,\n448\t\t\t\tCacheCreationTokens: cacheCreation,\n449\t\t\t\tSourceFile:          filename,\n450\t\t\t\tLineNumber:          lineNumber,\n451\t\t\t})\n452\t\n453\t\t\t// Batch insert every 100 events\n454\t\t\tif len(events) >= 100 {\n455\t\t\t\tif err := tc.cache.InsertTokenEventBatch(events); err != nil {\n456\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to insert batch for %s: %w\", filename, err)\n457\t\t\t\t}\n458\t\t\t\tevents = events[:0]\n459\t\t\t}\n460\t\t}\n461\t\n462\t\t// Insert remaining events\n463\t\tif len(events) > 0 {\n464\t\t\tif err := tc.cache.InsertTokenEventBatch(events); err != nil {\n465\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to insert final batch for %s: %w\", filename, err)\n466\t\t\t}\n467\t\t}\n468\t\n469\t\t// Update file state\n470\t\tif err := tc.cache.SetFileState(filename, lineNumber, fileInfo.ModTime()); err != nil {\n471\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to set file state for %s: %w\", filename, err)\n472\t\t}\n473\t\n474\t\treturn nil\n475\t}\n476\t\n477\t// findProjectDir finds the Claude project directory for the given working directory,\n478\t// searching across all configured roots.\n479\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) findProjectDir(cwd string) string {\n480\t\tprojectName := strings.ReplaceAll(cwd, \"/\", \"-\")\n481\t\tfor _, root := range tc.projectsDirs {\n482\t\t\tprojectPath := filepath.Join(root, projectName)\n483\t\t\tif _, err := os.Stat(projectPath); err == nil {\n484\t\t\t\treturn projectPath\n485\t\t\t}\n486\t\t}\n487\t\treturn \"\"\n488\t}\n489\t\n490\t// findAllProjectDirs returns all project directories found under all configured roots.\n491\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) findAllProjectDirs() ([]string, error) {\n492\t\tvar dirs []string\n493\t\tfor _, root := range tc.projectsDirs {\n494\t\t\tif root == \"\" {\n495\t\t\t\tcontinue\n496\t\t\t}\n497\t\t\tif _, err := os.Stat(root); os.IsNotExist(err) {\n498\t\t\t\tcontinue\n499\t\t\t}\n500\t\t\tentries, err := os.ReadDir(root)\n501\t\t\tif err != nil {\n502\t\t\t\tcontinue\n503\t\t\t}\n504\t\t\tfor _, entry := range entries {\n505\t\t\t\tif entry.IsDir() {\n506\t\t\t\t\tdirs = append(dirs, filepath.Join(root, entry.Name()))\n507\t\t\t\t}\n508\t\t\t}\n509\t\t}\n510\t\treturn dirs, nil\n511\t}\n512\t\n513\t// findJSONLFilesRecursive returns all *.jsonl files under dir, including subdirectories.\n514\t// This captures subagent files stored at <project>/<uuid>/subagents/agent-*.jsonl\n515\t// in addition to the top-level <project>/<uuid>.jsonl conversation files.\n516\tfunc findJSONLFilesRecursive(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n517\t\tvar files []string\n518\t\terr := filepath.Walk(dir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {\n519\t\t\tif err != nil {\n520\t\t\t\treturn nil\n521\t\t\t}\n522\t\t\tif !info.IsDir() && strings.HasSuffix(path, \".jsonl\") {\n523\t\t\t\tfiles = append(files, path)\n524\t\t\t}\n525\t\t\treturn nil\n526\t\t})\n527\t\treturn files, err\n528\t}\n529\t\n530\t// calculate60sRate calculates the token rate over the last 60 seconds\n531\tfunc (tc *TokenCollector) calculate60sRate(events []TimestampedTokens) float64 {\n532\t\tif len(events) == 0 {\n533\t\t\treturn 0\n534\t\t}\n535\t\n536\t\t// Get the most recent timestamp\n537\t\tlastTime := events[len(events)-1].Timestamp\n538\t\tcutoffTime := lastTime.Add(-60 * time.Second)\n539\t\n540\t\t// Sum tokens in the last 60 seconds\n541\t\tvar totalTokens int64\n542\t\tvar windowStart time.Time\n543\t\n544\t\tfor i := len(events) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n545\t\t\tif events[i].Timestamp.Before(cutoffTime) {\n546\t\t\t\tbreak\n547\t\t\t}\n548\t\t\ttotalTokens += events[i].Tokens\n549\t\t\twindowStart = events[i].Timestamp\n550\t\t}\n551\t\n552\t\t// Calculate rate (tokens per minute)\n553\t\tif totalTokens == 0 {\n554\t\t\treturn 0\n555\t\t}\n556\t\n557\t\tduration := lastTime.Sub(windowStart)\n558\t\tif duration <= 0 {\n559\t\t\treturn 0\n560\t\t}\n561\t\n562\t\tminutes := duration.Minutes()\n563\t\tif minutes == 0 {\n564\t\t\treturn 0\n565\t\t}\n566\t\n567\t\treturn float64(totalTokens) / minutes\n568\t}\n569\t\n570\t// ModelPricing contains pricing rates for a Claude model\n571\ttype ModelPricing struct 9am, returns last Monday's 9am\nfunc GetMondayNineAM() time.Time {\n\tnow := time.Now()\n\t// Find the most recent Monday\n\tweekday := int(now.Weekday())\n\tif weekday == 0 {\n\t\tweekday = 7 // Sunday becomes 7 for easier math\n\t}\n\tdaysUntilMonday := weekday - 1 // Days since Monday (Mon=0, Tue=1, ...)\n\n\t// Start of Monday (midnight)\n\tmonday := now.AddDate(0, 0, -daysUntilMonday)\n\tmonday = time.Date(monday.Year(), monday.Month(), monday.Day(), 9, 0, 0, 0, monday.Location())\n\n\t// If we haven't reached 9am on Monday yet, go back to previous Monday\n\tif NewTokenCollectorWithPath creates a TokenCollector with a custom path (for testing)\nfunc NewTokenCollectorWithPath(path string) *TokenCollector {\n\ttc := &TokenCollector{\n\t\tprojectsDirs: []string{path},\n\t\tlookbackFrom: GetMondayNineAM(),\n\t\tcache:        NewTokenCache(),\n\t}\n\ttc.startBackgroundIngestion()\n\treturn tc\n}\n\n// startBackgroundIngestion starts a goroutine that ingests JSONL files into SQLite\n// independently of the UI refresh cycle. This decouples slow file I/O from the\n// fast DB query that populates the token panel.\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) startBackgroundIngestion() {\n\ttc.stopIngestion = make(chan struct{})\n\tgo func() {\n\t\t// Run immediately so data is available as soon as possible\n\t\ttc.runIngestionCycle()\n\n\t\tticker := time.NewTicker(30 * time.Second)\n\t\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n\t\tfor {\n\t\t\tselect {\n\t\t\tcase <-tc.stopIngestion:\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n\t\t\t\ttc.runIngestionCycle()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n}\n\n// StopBackgroundIngestion shuts down the background ingestion goroutine.\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) StopBackgroundIngestion() {\n\tif tc.stopIngestion != nil {\n\t\tclose(tc.stopIngestion)\n\t\ttc.stopIngestion = nil\n\t}\n}\n\n// runIngestionCycle scans all JSONL files and ingests new data into SQLite.\n// Called by the background goroutine; uses ingestMu so it never blocks fast\n// cache/lease operations.\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) runIngestionCycle() {\n\tif len(tc.projectsDirs) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tprojectDirs, err := tc.findAllProjectDirs()\n\tif err != nil || len(projectDirs) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tvar files []string\n\tfor _, projectDir := range projectDirs {\n\t\tdirFiles, err := findJSONLFilesRecursive(projectDir)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tfiles = append(files, dirFiles...)\n\t}\n\n\tcompleteThreshold := GetFileCompleteThreshold()\n\tfor _, file := range files {\n\t\tfileInfo, err := os.Stat(file)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif agg, ok := tc.cache.GetFileAggregate(file); ok && agg.IsComplete {\n\t\t\tif !fileInfo.ModTime().After(agg.CompletedAt) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\ttc.cache.MarkFileActive(file)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif time.Since(fileInfo.ModTime()) > completeThreshold {\n\t\t\tif err := tc.ingestJSONLFile(file); err == nil {\n\t\t\t\ttc.cache.MarkFileComplete(file)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ttc.ingestJSONLFile(file)\n\t}\n}\n\n// AddProjectsDir adds an additional root directory to scan for JSONL files.\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) AddProjectsDir(path string) {\n\ttc.projectsDirs = append(tc.projectsDirs, path)\n}\n\n// SetLookback sets the lookback time filter\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) SetLookback(t time.Time) {\n\ttc.lookbackFrom = t\n}\n\n// GetLookback returns the current lookback time\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) GetLookback() time.Time {\n\treturn tc.lookbackFrom\n}\n\n// GetCache returns the underlying token cache for shared metrics operations\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) GetCache() *TokenCache {\n\treturn tc.cache\n}\n\n// claudeMessage represents the structure of Claude API messages in JSONL\ntype claudeMessage struct {\n\tMessage   messageData `json:\"message\"`\n\tTimestamp string      `json:\"timestamp\"`\n\tType      string      `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\n// messageData contains the actual API response\ntype messageData struct {\n\tModel string    `json:\"model\"`\n\tUsage usageData `json:\"usage\"`\n}\n\n// usageData contains token usage information\ntype usageData struct {\n\tInputTokens              int64         `json:\"input_tokens\"`\n\tCacheCreationInputTokens int64         `json:\"cache_creation_input_tokens\"`\n\tCacheReadInputTokens     int64         `json:\"cache_read_input_tokens\"`\n\tOutputTokens             int64         `json:\"output_tokens\"`\n\tCacheCreation            cacheCreation `json:\"cache_creation\"`\n}\n\n// cacheCreation contains detailed cache creation token breakdown\ntype cacheCreation struct {\n\tEphemeral5mInputTokens int64 `json:\"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens\"`\n\tEphemeral1hInputTokens int64 `json:\"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens\"`\n}\n\n// Collect returns token metrics from the SQLite cache. File ingestion runs in a\n// background goroutine (started by the constructor) so this method only executes\n// the fast DB query and never blocks on file I/O.\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) Collect() (*TokenMetrics, error) {\n\tmetrics := &TokenMetrics{\n\t\tAvailable:    false,\n\t\tLastUpdate:   time.Now(),\n\t\tLookbackFrom: tc.lookbackFrom,\n\t\tModels:       []string{},\n\t}\n\n\tif len(tc.projectsDirs) == 0 {\n\t\tmetrics.Error = \"No projects directories configured\"\n\t\treturn metrics, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Query SQLite using hybrid approach (pre-aggregated + active events)\n\taggregated, err := tc.cache.QueryTokensHybrid(tc.lookbackFrom)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tmetrics.Error = fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to query token cache: %v\", err)\n\t\treturn metrics, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Populate metrics from query results\n\tmetrics.InputTokens = aggregated.InputTokens\n\tmetrics.OutputTokens = aggregated.OutputTokens\n\tmetrics.CacheReadTokens = aggregated.CacheReadTokens\n\tmetrics.CacheCreationTokens = aggregated.CacheCreationTokens\n\tmetrics.TotalTokens = aggregated.InputTokens + aggregated.OutputTokens +\n\t\taggregated.CacheReadTokens + aggregated.CacheCreationTokens\n\tmetrics.Prompts = aggregated.EventCount\n\tmetrics.EarliestTimestamp = aggregated.EarliestTimestamp\n\tmetrics.LatestTimestamp = aggregated.LatestTimestamp\n\n\tif !aggregated.EarliestTimestamp.IsZero() && !aggregated.LatestTimestamp.IsZero() {\n\t\tmetrics.TimeSpan = aggregated.LatestTimestamp.Sub(aggregated.EarliestTimestamp)\n\t}\n\n\t// Build model list and per-model usage\n\tvar totalCost float64\n\tmetrics.ModelUsages = make([]ModelUsage, 0, len(aggregated.ModelMetrics))\n\n\tfor model, mm := range aggregated.ModelMetrics {\n\t\tmetrics.Models = append(metrics.Models, model)\n\n\t\tpricing := getPricingForModel(model)\n\t\tinputCost := float64(mm.InputTokens) * pricing.InputPerMillion / 1_000_000\n\t\toutputCost := float64(mm.OutputTokens) * pricing.OutputPerMillion / 1_000_000\n\t\tcacheReadCost := float64(mm.CacheReadTokens) * pricing.CacheReadPerMillion / 1_000_000\n\t\tcacheCreateCost := float64(mm.CacheCreationTokens) * pricing.CacheCreatePerMillion / 1_000_000\n\t\tmodelCost := inputCost + outputCost + cacheReadCost + cacheCreateCost\n\n\t\tusage := ModelUsage{\n\t\t\tModel:               model,\n\t\t\tInputTokens:         mm.InputTokens,\n\t\t\tOutputTokens:        mm.OutputTokens,\n\t\t\tCacheReadTokens:     mm.CacheReadTokens,\n\t\t\tCacheCreationTokens: mm.CacheCreationTokens,\n\t\t\tTotalTokens:         mm.InputTokens + mm.OutputTokens + mm.CacheReadTokens + mm.CacheCreationTokens,\n\t\t\tCost:                modelCost,\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetrics.ModelUsages = append(metrics.ModelUsages, usage)\n\t\ttotalCost += modelCost\n\t}\n\n\tsort.Strings(metrics.Models)\n\n\t// Sort model usages by cost (highest first)\n\tsort.Slice(metrics.ModelUsages, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\treturn metrics.ModelUsages[i].Cost > metrics.ModelUsages[j].Cost\n\t})\n\n\tmetrics.TotalCost = totalCost\n\n\t// Calculate session average rate\n\tif metrics.TimeSpan > 0 {\n\t\tminutes := metrics.TimeSpan.Minutes()\n\t\tif minutes > 0 {\n\t\t\tmetrics.SessionAvgRate = float64(metrics.TotalTokens) / minutes\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Calculate 60-second window rate from recent events\n\trecentEvents, err := tc.cache.QueryRecentEvents(60)\n\tif err == nil && len(recentEvents) > 0 {\n\t\tmetrics.Rate = tc.calculate60sRate(recentEvents)\n\t}\n\n\tmetrics.Available = true\n\treturn metrics, nil\n}\n\n// ingestJSONLFile reads a JSONL file and inserts new events into SQLite\n// Returns an error if database operations fail (for proper error handling)\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) ingestJSONLFile(filename string) error {\n\tif tc.cache == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Check file modification time\n\tfileInfo, err := os.Stat(filename)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil // File may have been deleted, not a critical error\n\t}\n\n\t// Get last processed state\n\tlastLine, lastMod, exists := tc.cache.GetFileState(filename)\n\n\t// If file hasn't been modified since last processing, skip\n\tif exists && !fileInfo.ModTime().After(lastMod) {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\t// If file was modified (truncated/rewritten), invalidate and reprocess\n\tif exists && fileInfo.ModTime().After(lastMod) {\n\t\t// Check if file was truncated (new size < last line count implies rewrite)\n\t\t// For safety, we'll just process from where we left off\n\t\t// but if file was completely rewritten, invalidate\n\t\tfile, err := os.Open(filename)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil // File may have been deleted\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer file.Close()\n\n\t\t// Count current lines\n\t\tvar currentLineCount int64\n\t\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(file)\n\t\tbuf := make([]byte, 0, 1024*1024)\n\t\tscanner.Buffer(buf, 10*1024*1024)\n\t\tfor scanner.Scan() {\n\t\t\tcurrentLineCount++\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If file has fewer lines than we processed, it was rewritten\n\t\tif currentLineCount < lastLine {\n\t\t\tif err := tc.cache.InvalidateFile(filename); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to invalidate file %s: %w\", filename, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tlastLine = 0\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Open file for processing\n\tfile, err := os.Open(filename)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil // File may have been deleted\n\t}\n\tdefer file.Close()\n\n\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(file)\n\tbuf := make([]byte, 0, 1024*1024)\n\tscanner.Buffer(buf, 10*1024*1024)\n\n\tvar lineNumber int64\n\tvar events []TokenEvent\n\n\tfor scanner.Scan() {\n\t\tlineNumber++\n\n\t\t// Skip already processed lines\n\t\tif lineNumber <= lastLine {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar msg claudeMessage\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(scanner.Bytes(), &msg); err != nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Only process assistant messages (count all requests, even with zero tokens)\n\t\tif msg.Type != \"assistant\" {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Parse timestamp\n\t\ttimestamp, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339Nano, msg.Timestamp)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tusage := msg.Message.Usage\n\t\tcacheCreation := usage.CacheCreationInputTokens\n\t\tif cacheCreation == 0 {\n\t\t\tcacheCreation = usage.CacheCreation.Ephemeral5mInputTokens +\n\t\t\t\tusage.CacheCreation.Ephemeral1hInputTokens\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tevents = append(events, TokenEvent{\n\t\t\tTimestamp:           timestamp,\n\t\t\tModel:               msg.Message.Model,\n\t\t\tInputTokens:         usage.InputTokens,\n\t\t\tOutputTokens:        usage.OutputTokens,\n\t\t\tCacheReadTokens:     usage.CacheReadInputTokens,\n\t\t\tCacheCreationTokens: cacheCreation,\n\t\t\tSourceFile:          filename,\n\t\t\tLineNumber:          lineNumber,\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Batch insert every 100 events\n\t\tif len(events) >= 100 {\n\t\t\tif err := tc.cache.InsertTokenEventBatch(events); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to insert batch for %s: %w\", filename, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tevents = events[:0]\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Insert remaining events\n\tif len(events) > 0 {\n\t\tif err := tc.cache.InsertTokenEventBatch(events); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to insert final batch for %s: %w\", filename, err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Update file state\n\tif err := tc.cache.SetFileState(filename, lineNumber, fileInfo.ModTime()); err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to set file state for %s: %w\", filename, err)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// findProjectDir finds the Claude project directory for the given working directory,\n// searching across all configured roots.\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) findProjectDir(cwd string) string {\n\tprojectName := strings.ReplaceAll(cwd, \"/\", \"-\")\n\tfor _, root := range tc.projectsDirs {\n\t\tprojectPath := filepath.Join(root, projectName)\n\t\tif _, err := os.Stat(projectPath); err == nil {\n\t\t\treturn projectPath\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn \"\"\n}\n\n// findAllProjectDirs returns all project directories found under all configured roots.\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) findAllProjectDirs() ([]string, error) {\n\tvar dirs []string\n\tfor _, root := range tc.projectsDirs {\n\t\tif root == \"\" {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tif _, err := os.Stat(root); os.IsNotExist(err) {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tentries, err := os.ReadDir(root)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, entry := range entries {\n\t\t\tif entry.IsDir() {\n\t\t\t\tdirs = append(dirs, filepath.Join(root, entry.Name()))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn dirs, nil\n}\n\n// findJSONLFilesRecursive returns all *.jsonl files under dir, including subdirectories.\n// This captures subagent files stored at <project>/<uuid>/subagents/agent-*.jsonl\n// in addition to the top-level <project>/<uuid>.jsonl conversation files.\nfunc findJSONLFilesRecursive(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n\tvar files []string\n\terr := filepath.Walk(dir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !info.IsDir() && strings.HasSuffix(path, \".jsonl\") {\n\t\t\tfiles = append(files, path)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil\n\t})\n\treturn files, err\n}\n\n// calculate60sRate calculates the token rate over the last 60 seconds\nfunc (tc *TokenCollector) calculate60sRate(events []TimestampedTokens) float64 {\n\tif len(events) == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n\n\t// Get the most recent timestamp\n\tlastTime := events[len(events)-1].Timestamp\n\tcutoffTime := lastTime.Add(-60 * time.Second)\n\n\t// Sum tokens in the last 60 seconds\n\tvar totalTokens int64\n\tvar windowStart time.Time\n\n\tfor i := len(events) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n\t\tif events[i].Timestamp.Before(cutoffTime) {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\ttotalTokens += events[i].Tokens\n\t\twindowStart = events[i].Timestamp\n\t}\n\n\t// Calculate rate (tokens per minute)\n\tif totalTokens == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n\n\tduration := lastTime.Sub(windowStart)\n\tif duration <= 0 {\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n\n\tminutes := duration.Minutes()\n\tif minutes == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n\n\treturn float64(totalTokens) / minutes\n}\n\n// ModelPricing contains pricing rates time.Hour)\n101\t\t\t\t},\n102\t\t\t},\n103\t\t\t{\n104\t\t\t\tName:        \"24 hours\",\n105\t\t\t\tDescription: \"Last 24 hours\",\n106\t\t\t\tGetTime: func() time.Time {\n107\t\t\t\t\treturn {\n114\t\t\t\t\treturn time.Now().AddDate(0, 0, -7)\n115\t\t\t\t},\n116\t\t\t},\n117\t\t\t{\n118\t\t\t\tName:        \"30 days\",\n119\t\t\t\tDescription: \"Last 30 days\",\n120\t\t\t\tGetTime: func() data\",\n127\t\t\t\tGetTime: func() time.Time {\n128\t\t\t\t\treturn time.Time{} // Zero time = no filter\n129\t\t\t\t},\n130\t\t\t},\n131\t\t\t{\n132\t\t\t\tName:        \"Custom...\",\n133\t\t\t\tDescription: \"Set a custom date and time\",\n134\t\t\t\tGetTime:     nil, // Special case: opens custom picker\n135\t\t\t},\n136\t\t}\n137\t\n138\t\treturn &Dashboard{\n139\t\t\tversion:            version,\n140\t\t\tinstanceID:         generateInstanceID(),\n141\t\t\tsystemCollector:    metrics.NewSystemCollector(),\n142\t\t\ttokenCollector: time.Now(),\n146\t\t\tlookbackPresets:    presets,\n147\t\t\tlookbackCustomDate: time.Now().AddDate(0, 0, -1), // Default custom to yesterday\n148\t\t}\n149\t}\n150\t\n151\t// AddProjectsDirs adds {\n161\t\treturn tea.Batch(\n162\t\t\td.tick(),\n163\t\t\td.collectMetrics(),\n164\t\t\td.checkForUpdates(),\n165\t\t)\n166\t}\n167\t\n168\t// updateCheckMsg carries update check results\n169\ttype error\n176\t}\n177\t\n178\t// checkForUpdates returns a command that checks for updates\n179\tfunc (d *Dashboard) checkForUpdates() tea.Cmd {\n180\t\treturn func() tea.Msg {\n181\t\t\tinfo := d.updater.CheckForUpdate()\n182\t\t\treturn updateCheckMsg{info: info}\n183\t\t}\n184\t}\n185\t\n186\t// Update handles messages\n187\tfunc (d *Dashboard) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {\n188\t\tswitch msg := msg.(type) {\n189\t\tcase tea.WindowSizeMsg:\n190\t\t\td.width = msg.Width\n191\t\t\td.height = msg.Height\n192\t\t\td.updateLayout()\n193\t\t\treturn d, nil\n194\t\n195\t\tcase tea.KeyMsg:\n196\t\t\t// Handle lookback picker mode\n197\t\t\tif d.lookbackMode {\n198\t\t\t\treturn d.handleLookbackKey(msg)\n199\t\t\t}\n200\t\n201\t\t\tswitch msg.String() {\n202\t\t\tcase \"q\", \"ctrl+c\":\n203\t\t\t\treturn d, tea.Quit\n204\t\t\tcase \"r\":\n205\t\t\t\treturn d, d.collectMetrics()\n206\t\t\tcase \"h\":\n207\t\t\t\t// Cycle through help modes: 0 -> 1 -> 2 -> 3 -> 0\n208\t\t\t\td.helpMode = (d.helpMode + 1) % 4\n209\t\t\t\treturn d, nil\n210\t\t\tcase \"l\", \"L\":\n211\t\t\t\t// Open lookback picker\n212\t\t\t\td.lookbackMode = true\n213\t\t\t\td.helpMode = 0 // Close help if open\n214\t\t\t\treturn d, nil\n215\t\t\tcase \"u\", \"U\":\n216\t\t\t\t// Perform update if available\n217\t\t\t\tif d.updateInfo != nil && d.updateInfo.UpdateAvailable && !d.updating {\n218\t\t\t\t\td.updating = true\n219\t\t\t\t\td.updateStatus = \"Downloading update...\"\n220\t\t\t\t\treturn d, d.performUpdate()\n221\t\t\t\t}\n222\t\t\t\treturn d, nil\n223\t\t\t}\n224\t\n225\t\tcase tickMsg:\n226\t\t\treturn d, tea.Batch(d.tick(), d.collectMetrics(), d.checkForUpdates())\n227\t\n228\t\tcase metricsMsg:\n229\t\t\td.systemMetrics = msg.system\n230\t\t\td.tokenMetrics = msg.tokens\n231\t\t\td.tmuxMetrics = msg.tmux\n232\t\t\td.lastUpdate = time.Now()\n233\t\t\treturn d, nil\n234\t\n235\t\tcase updateCheckMsg:\n236\t\t\td.updateInfo = msg.info\n237\t\t\treturn d, nil\n238\t\n239\t\tcase updateCompleteMsg:\n240\t\t\td.updating = false\n241\t\t\tif msg.err != nil {\n242\t\t\t\td.updateStatus = fmt.Sprintf(\"Update failed: %v\", msg.err)\n243\t\t\t} else {\n244\t\t\t\td.updateStatus = \"Update complete! Restarting...\"\n245\t\t\t\t// The app should restart automatically\n246\t\t\t\treturn d, tea.Quit\n247\t\t\t}\n248\t\t\treturn d, nil\n249\t\n250\t\tcase errMsg:\n251\t\t\td.err = msg.err\n252\t\t\treturn d, nil\n253\t\t}\n254\t\n255\t\treturn d, nil\n256\t}\n257\t\n258\t// performUpdate returns a command that applies the update\n259\tfunc (d *Dashboard) performUpdate() tea.Cmd {\n260\t\treturn func() tea.Msg {\n261\t\t\terr := d.updater.PerformUpdateWithRestart(d.updateInfo)\n262\t\t\treturn updateCompleteMsg{err: err}\n263\t\t}\n264\t}\n265\t\n266\t// handleLookbackKey handles keyboard input when lookback picker is open\n267\tfunc (d *Dashboard) handleLookbackKey(msg tea.KeyMsg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {\n268\t\tif d.lookbackCustomMode {\n269\t\t\t// Custom date/time editing mode\n270\t\t\tswitch msg.String() {\n271\t\t\tcase \"esc\":\n272\t\t\t\td.lookbackCustomMode = false\n273\t\t\t\treturn d, nil\n274\t\t\tcase \"enter\":\n275\t\t\t\t// Apply custom date and close picker\n276\t\t\t\td.tokenCollector.SetLookback(d.lookbackCustomDate)\n277\t\t\t\td.lookbackCustomMode = false\n278\t\t\t\td.lookbackMode = false\n279\t\t\t\treturn d, d.collectMetrics()\n280\t\t\tcase \"tab\", \"right\":\n281\t\t\t\td.lookbackEditField = (d.lookbackEditField + 1) % 5\n282\t\t\t\treturn d, nil\n283\t\t\tcase \"shift+tab\", \"left\":\n284\t\t\t\td.lookbackEditField = (d.lookbackEditField + 4) % 5\n285\t\t\t\treturn d, nil\n286\t\t\tcase \"up\":\n287\t\t\t\td.adjustCustomDate(1)\n288\t\t\t\treturn d, nil\n289\t\t\tcase \"down\":\n290\t\t\t\td.adjustCustomDate(-1)\n291\t\t\t\treturn d, nil\n292\t\t\t}\n293\t\t\treturn d, nil\n294\t\t}\n295\t\n296\t\t// Preset selection mode\n297\t\tswitch msg.String() {\n298\t\tcase \"esc\", \"l\", \"q\":\n299\t\t\td.lookbackMode = false\n300\t\t\treturn d, nil\n301\t\tcase \"up\", \"k\":\n302\t\t\tif d.lookbackSelectedIndex > 0 {\n303\t\t\t\td.lookbackSelectedIndex--\n304\t\t\t}\n305\t\t\treturn d, nil\n306\t\tcase \"down\", \"j\":\n307\t\t\tif d.lookbackSelectedIndex < len(d.lookbackPresets)-1 {\n308\t\t\t\td.lookbackSelectedIndex++\n309\t\t\t}\n310\t\t\treturn d, nil\n311\t\tcase \"enter\", \" \":\n312\t\t\tpreset := d.lookbackPresets[d.lookbackSelectedIndex]\n313\t\t\tif preset.GetTime == nil {\n314\t\t\t\t// Custom mode - enter custom date picker\n315\t\t\t\td.lookbackCustomMode = true\n316\t\t\t\td.lookbackEditField = 0\n317\t\t\t\treturn d, nil\n318\t\t\t}\n319\t\t\t// Apply preset and close picker\n320\t\t\td.tokenCollector.SetLookback(preset.GetTime())\n321\t\t\td.lookbackMode = false\n322\t\t\treturn d, d.collectMetrics()\n323\t\t}\n324\t\treturn d, nil\n325\t}\n326\t\n327\t// adjustCustomDate adjusts the custom date based on current edit field\n328\tfunc (d *Dashboard) adjustCustomDate(delta int) {\n329\t\tswitch d.lookbackEditField {\n330\t\tcase 0: // Year\n331\t\t\td.lookbackCustomDate = d.lookbackCustomDate.AddDate(delta, 0, 0)\n332\t\tcase 1: // Month\n333\t\t\td.lookbackCustomDate = d.lookbackCustomDate.AddDate(0, delta, 0)\n334\t\tcase 2: // Day\n335\t\t\td.lookbackCustomDate = d.lookbackCustomDate.AddDate(0, 0, delta)\n336\t\tcase 3: // Hour\n337\t\t\td.lookbackCustomDate = d.lookbackCustomDate.Add(time.Duration(delta) * time.Hour)\n338\t\tcase 4: // Minute\n339\t\t\td.lookbackCustomDate = d.lookbackCustomDate.Add(time.Duration(delta) * time.Minute)\n340\t\t}\n341\t\n342\t\t// Clamp to not be in the future\n343\t\tif d.lookbackCustomDate.After(time.Now()) {\n344\t\t\td.lookbackCustomDate = time.Now()\n345\t\t}\n346\t}\n347\t\n348\t// View renders the dashboard\n349\tfunc (d *Dashboard) View() string {\n350\t\tif d.width == 0 {\n351\t\t\treturn \"Initializing...\"\n352\t\t}\n353\t\n354\t\tvar content string\n355\t\n356\t\t// Check if in lookback picker mode\n357\t\tif d.lookbackMode {\n358\t\t\tcontent = d.renderLookbackPicker()\n359\t\t} else if d.helpMode > 0 {\n360\t\t\t// Check if in help mode\n361\t\t\tcontent = d.renderHelpView()\n362\t\t} else {\n363\t\t\tswitch d.layoutMode {\n364\t\t\tcase LayoutUltraWide:\n365\t\t\t\tcontent = d.renderUltraWide()\n366\t\t\tcase LayoutWide:\n367\t\t\t\tcontent = d.renderWide()\n368\t\t\tcase LayoutCompact:\n369\t\t\t\tcontent = d.renderCompact()\n370\t\t\tdefault:\n371\t\t\t\tcontent = d.renderNarrow()\n372\t\t\t}\n373\t\t}\n374\t\n375\t\t// Add status bar\n376\t\tstatusBar := d.renderStatusBar()\n377\t\n378\t\t// Join content and status bar\n379\t\toutput := lipgloss.JoinVertical(lipgloss.Left, content, statusBar)\n380\t\n381\t\t// CRITICAL: Ensure output fills the entire terminal height to prevent\n382\t\t// external process output (like Tailscale logs) from bleeding through\n383\t\t// at the bottom of the screen. Without this, the alternate screen buffer\n384\t\t// may show underlying terminal content in unfilled rows.\n385\t\toutputHeight := lipgloss.Height(output)\n386\t\tif outputHeight < d.height {\n387\t\t\t// Pad with empty lines to fill the screen\n388\t\t\tpadding := strings.Repeat(\"\\n\", d.height-outputHeight-1)\n389\t\t\toutput = output + padding\n390\t\t}\n391\t\n392\t\treturn output\n393\t}\n394\t\n395\t// updateLayout determines the current layout mode based on terminal size\n396\tfunc (d *Dashboard) updateLayout() {\n397\t\tif d.width < 120 {\n398\t\t\t// Compact stacked layout: tmux top, tokens middle, system bottom\n399\t\t\td.layoutMode = LayoutCompact\n400\t\t} else {\n401\t\t\t// Always use 3-column layout for wide terminals\n402\t\t\td.layoutMode = LayoutUltraWide\n403\t\t}\n404\t}\n405\t\n406\t// tick returns a command that sends a tick message every 2 seconds\n407\tfunc (d *Dashboard) tick() tea.Cmd {\n408\t\treturn tea.Tick(2*time.Second, func(t time.Time) tea.Msg {\n409\t\t\treturn tickMsg(t)\n410\t\t})\n411\t}\n412\t\n413\t// metricsMsg carries collected metrics\n414\ttype metricsMsg struct {\n415\t\tsystem metrics.SystemMetrics\n416\t\ttokens *metrics.TokenMetrics\n417\t\ttmux   *metrics.TmuxMetrics\n418\t}\n419\t\n420\t// errMsg carries errors\n421\ttype errMsg struct {\n422\t\terr error\n423\t}\n424\t\n425\t// Metric type constants for cache keys\n426\tconst (\n427\t\tmetricTypeSystem = \"system\"\n428\t\tmetricTypeTmux   = \"tmux\"\n429\t)\n430\t\n431\t// collectMetrics returns a command that collects all metrics\n432\t// Uses leader election: only one instance collects, others read from cache\n433\tfunc (d *Dashboard) collectMetrics() tea.Cmd {\n434\t\treturn func() tea.Msg {\n435\t\t\tcache := d.tokenCollector.GetCache()\n436\t\t\tisLeader := cache.TryAcquireLease(d.instanceID)\n437\t\n438\t\t\tvar system metrics.SystemMetrics\n439\t\t\tvar tokens *metrics.TokenMetrics\n440\t\t\tvar tmux *metrics.TmuxMetrics\n441\t\n442\t\t\t// Use channels to collect results with timeout\n443\t\t\ttype systemResult struct {\n444\t\t\t\tmetrics metrics.SystemMetrics\n445\t\t\t}\n446\t\t\ttype tokenResult struct {\n447\t\t\t\tmetrics *metrics.TokenMetrics\n448\t\t\t}\n449\t\t\ttype tmuxResult struct {\n450\t\t\t\tmetrics *metrics.TmuxMetrics\n451\t\t\t}\n452\t\n453\t\t\tsystemChan := make(chan systemResult, 1)\n454\t\t\ttokenChan := make(chan tokenResult, 1)\n455\t\t\ttmuxChan := make(chan tmuxResult, 1)\n456\t\n457\t\t\t// System metrics: try cache first, collect if leader or cache miss\n458\t\t\tgo func() {\n459\t\t\t\tif !isLeader {\n460\t\t\t\t\tif data, ok := cache.GetCachedMetrics(metricTypeSystem); ok {\n461\t\t\t\t\t\tvar cached metrics.SystemMetrics\n462\t\t\t\t\t\tif json.Unmarshal(data, &cached) == nil {\n463\t\t\t\t\t\t\tsystemChan <- systemResult{metrics: cached}\n464\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn\n465\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n466\t\t\t\t\t}\n467\t\t\t\t}\n468\t\t\t\t// Leader or cache miss: collect fresh\n469\t\t\t\tm := d.systemCollector.Collect()\n470\t\t\t\tif isLeader {\n471\t\t\t\t\tif data, err := json.Marshal(m); err == nil {\n472\t\t\t\t\t\tcache.SetCachedMetrics(metricTypeSystem, data)\n473\t\t\t\t\t}\n474\t\t\t\t}\n475\t\t\t\tsystemChan <- systemResult{metrics: m}\n476\t\t\t}()\n477\t\n478\t\t\t// Token metrics: always collect (uses shared DB, cheap to query)\n479\t\t\tgo func() {\n480\t\t\t\tt, _ := d.tokenCollector.Collect()\n481\t\t\t\ttokenChan <- tokenResult{metrics: t}\n482\t\t\t}()\n483\t\n484\t\t\t// Tmux metrics: try cache first, collect if leader or cache miss\n485\t\t\tgo func() {\n486\t\t\t\tif !isLeader {\n487\t\t\t\t\tif data, ok := cache.GetCachedMetrics(metricTypeTmux); ok {\n488\t\t\t\t\t\tvar cached metrics.TmuxMetrics\n489\t\t\t\t\t\tif json.Unmarshal(data, &cached) == nil {\n490\t\t\t\t\t\t\ttmuxChan <- tmuxResult{metrics: &cached}\n491\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn\n492\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n493\t\t\t\t\t}\n494\t\t\t\t}\n495\t\t\t\t// Leader or cache miss: collect fresh\n496\t\t\t\tm := d.tmuxCollector.Collect()\n497\t\t\t\tif isLeader {\n498\t\t\t\t\tif data, err := json.Marshal(m); err == nil {\n499\t\t\t\t\t\tcache.SetCachedMetrics(metricTypeTmux, data)\n500\t\t\t\t\t}\n501\t\t\t\t}\n502\t\t\t\ttmuxChan <- tmuxResult{metrics: m}\n503\t\t\t}()\n504\t\n505\t\t\t// Wait for results with 3 second timeout\n506\t\t\ttimeout := time.After(3 * time.Second)\n507\t\n508\t\t\t// Collect results as they come in, or timeout\n509\t\t\tfor i := 0; i < 3; i++ {\n510\t\t\t\tselect {\n511\t\t\t\tcase r := <-systemChan:\n512\t\t\t\t\tsystem = r.metrics\n513\t\t\t\tcase r := <-tokenChan:\n514\t\t\t\t\ttokens = r.metrics\n515\t\t\t\tcase r := <-tmuxChan:\n516\t\t\t\t\ttmux = r.metrics\n517\t\t\t\tcase <-timeout:\n518\t\t\t\t\t// Return whatever we have so far\n519\t\t\t\t\treturn metricsMsg{\n520\t\t\t\t\t\tsystem: system,\n521\t\t\t\t\t\ttokens: tokens,\n522\t\t\t\t\t\ttmux:   tmux,\n523\t\t\t\t\t}\n524\t\t\t\t}\n525\t\t\t}\n526\t\n527\t\t\treturn metricsMsg{\n528\t\t\t\tsystem: system,\n529\t\t\t\ttokens: tokens,\n530\t\t\t\ttmux:   tmux,\n531\t\t\t}\n532\t\t}\n533\t}\n534\t\n535\t// calculateTokenPanelWidth determines the optimal width for the token panel\n536\t// based on actual content needs, returning the minimum width that displays well\n537\tfunc (d *Dashboard) calculateTokenPanelWidth() int {\n538\t\t// Base minimum for the panel structure (stacked layout)\n539\t\tminWidth := 46\n540\t\n541\t\t// If no token metrics or not available, use minimum\n542\t\tif d.tokenMetrics == nil || !d.tokenMetrics.Available {\n543\t\t\treturn minWidth\n544\t\t}\n545\t\n546\t\tmodelCount := len(d.tokenMetrics.ModelUsages)\n547\t\n548\t\t// Side-by-side layout needs:\n549\t\t// - Left column: 22 chars (stats)\n550\t\t// - Separator: 2 chars\n551\t\t// - Right column: ~24 chars (model name + cost)\n552\t\t// - Borders/padding: 4 chars\n553\t\t// Total: ~52 chars minimum for side-by-side\n554\t\tif modelCount > 0 {\n555\t\t\t// With models, use side-by-side layout\n556\t\t\t// More models = need slightly more height but same width\n557\t\t\treturn 54\n558\t\t}\n559\t\n560\t\t// Just basic token counts, no models - use narrow layout\n561\t\treturn minWidth\n562\t}\n563\t\n564\t// calculateTmuxPanelWidth determines the width needed for the TMUX panel\n565\t// based on session count and available height (to calculate columns needed)\n566\tfunc (d *Dashboard) calculateTmuxPanelWidth(panelHeight int) int {\n567\t\tconst minCellWidth = 28 // Minimum readable session cell\n568\t\tconst minWidth = 50     // Absolute minimum for 1 column\n569\t\tconst maxWidth = 120    // Cap to prevent TMUX from taking too much space\n570\t\n571\t\t// If no tmux metrics, use minimum\n572\t\tif d.tmuxMetrics == nil || !d.tmuxMetrics.Available {\n573\t\t\treturn minWidth\n574\t\t}\n575\t\n576\t\tsessionCount := len(d.tmuxMetrics.Sessions)\n577\t\tif sessionCount == 0 {\n578\t\t\treturn minWidth\n579\t\t}\n580\t\n581\t\t// Available lines for sessions: height - title(1) - borders(2)\n582\t\tavailableLines := panelHeight - 3\n583\t\tif availableLines < 1 {\n584\t\t\tavailableLines = 1\n585\t\t}\n586\t\n587\t\t// Calculate columns needed to fit all sessions\n588\t\tcols := 1\n589\t\tif sessionCount > availableLines {\n590\t\t\tcols = (sessionCount + availableLines - 1) / availableLines // ceil division\n591\t\t}\n592\t\tif cols > 4 {\n593\t\t\tcols = 4 // Reasonable maximum for readability\n594\t\t}\n595\t\n596\t\t// Width needed: columns * cellWidth + separators + borders/padding\n597\t\t// contentWidth = cols * cellWidth + (cols - 1) for separators\n598\t\t// panelWidth = contentWidth + 4 for borders/padding\n599\t\tneededWidth := cols*minCellWidth + (cols - 1) + 4\n600\t\n601\t\tif neededWidth < minWidth {\n602\t\t\treturn minWidth\n603\t\t}\n604\t\tif neededWidth > maxWidth {\n605\t\t\treturn maxWidth\n606\t\t}\n607\t\treturn neededWidth\n608\t}\n609\t\n610\t// getTmuxColumnCount returns the number of columns needed to display all sessions\n611\tfunc (d *Dashboard) getTmuxColumnCount(panelHeight int) int {\n612\t\tif d.tmuxMetrics == nil || !d.tmuxMetrics.Available {\n613\t\t\treturn 1\n614\t\t}\n615\t\n616\t\tsessionCount := len(d.tmuxMetrics.Sessions)\n617\t\tif sessionCount == 0 {\n618\t\t\treturn 1\n619\t\t}\n620\t\n621\t\tavailableLines := panelHeight - 3\n622\t\tif availableLines < 1 {\n623\t\t\tavailableLines = 1\n624\t\t}\n625\t\n626\t\tcols := 1\n627\t\tif sessionCount > availableLines {\n628\t\t\tcols = (sessionCount + availableLines - 1) / availableLines\n629\t\t}\n630\t\tif cols > 4 {\n631\t\t\tcols = 4\n632\t\t}\n633\t\treturn cols\n634\t}\n635\t\n636\t// renderUltraWide renders 3 panels side-by-side\n637\t// Balances space between Token and TMUX panels based on content needs\n638\tfunc (d *Dashboard) renderUltraWide() string {\n639\t\t// Account for panel padding (0,1) which adds 2 chars per panel = 6 total\n640\t\ttotalPanelWidth := d.width - 6\n641\t\tpanelHeight := d.height - 3 // -2 borders, -1 status line\n642\t\n643\t\t// Step 1: System panel gets fixed width for CPU bars\n644\t\tsystemWidth := 60\n645\t\tif totalPanelWidth < 180 {\n646\t\t\tsystemWidth = 55\n647\t\t}\n648\t\n649\t\t// Step 2: Calculate minimum and ideal widths for both panels\n650\t\tminTokenWidth := 46\n651\t\tminTmuxWidth := d.calculateTmuxPanelWidth(panelHeight)\n652\t\n653\t\t// Ideal token width: side-by-side layout with comfortable model display\n654\t\t// Left column (22) + separator (2) + right column for models\n655\t\t// Right column needs: model name (up to 15) + cost (8) + tokens (12) = ~35\n656\t\t// Total ideal: 22 + 2 + 35 + 4 (borders) = 60\n657\t\tidealTokenWidth := 60\n658\t\n659\t\t// Ideal tmux width: minimum cell width + some padding for session names\n660\t\t// Use 35 chars per cell (28 min + 7 for longer names)\n661\t\tidealCellWidth := 35\n662\t\ttmuxCols := d.getTmuxColumnCount(panelHeight)\n663\t\tidealTmuxWidth := tmuxCols*idealCellWidth + (tmuxCols - 1) + 4\n664\t\n665\t\t// Available space after system panel\n666\t\tavailableWidth := totalPanelWidth - systemWidth\n667\t\n668\t\t// Start with minimums\n669\t\ttokenWidth := minTokenWidth\n670\t\ttmuxWidth := minTmuxWidth\n671\t\n672\t\t// Calculate how much each panel wants beyond minimum\n673\t\ttokenWant := idealTokenWidth - minTokenWidth\n674\t\tif tokenWant < 0 {\n675\t\t\ttokenWant = 0\n676\t\t}\n677\t\ttmuxWant := idealTmuxWidth - minTmuxWidth\n678\t\tif tmuxWant < 0 {\n679\t\t\ttmuxWant = 0\n680\t\t}\n681\t\n682\t\t// Distribute remaining space proportionally based on wants\n683\t\tremainingAfterMins := availableWidth - minTokenWidth - minTmuxWidth\n684\t\tif remainingAfterMins > 0 {\n685\t\t\ttotalWant := tokenWant + tmuxWant\n686\t\t\tif totalWant > 0 {\n687\t\t\t\t// Proportional allocation\n688\t\t\t\ttokenExtra := remainingAfterMins * tokenWant / totalWant\n689\t\t\t\ttmuxExtra := remainingAfterMins - tokenExtra\n690\t\t\t\ttokenWidth = minTokenWidth + tokenExtra\n691\t\t\t\ttmuxWidth = minTmuxWidth + tmuxExtra\n692\t\t\t} else {\n693\t\t\t\t// Neither wants more, split evenly\n694\t\t\t\ttokenWidth = minTokenWidth + remainingAfterMins/2\n695\t\t\t\ttmuxWidth = minTmuxWidth + remainingAfterMins - remainingAfterMins/2\n696\t\t\t}\n697\t\t} else if remainingAfterMins < 0 {\n698\t\t\t// Not enough space for both minimums - compress proportionally\n699\t\t\tdeficit := -remainingAfterMins\n700\t\t\ttotalMin := minTokenWidth + minTmuxWidth\n701\t\t\t// Reduce each panel proportionally to its minimum\n702\t\t\ttokenReduction := deficit * minTokenWidth / totalMin\n703\t\t\ttmuxReduction := deficit - tokenReduction\n704\t\t\ttokenWidth = minTokenWidth - tokenReduction\n705\t\t\ttmuxWidth = minTmuxWidth - tmuxReduction\n706\t\t\t// Enforce absolute minimums\n707\t\t\tif tokenWidth < 30 {\n708\t\t\t\ttokenWidth = 30\n709\t\t\t\ttmuxWidth = availableWidth - tokenWidth\n710\t\t\t}\n711\t\t\tif tmuxWidth < 30 {\n712\t\t\t\ttmuxWidth = 30\n713\t\t\t\ttokenWidth = availableWidth - tmuxWidth\n714\t\t\t}\n715\t\t}\n716\t\n717\t\t// Cap token panel - it doesn't need more than ideal\n718\t\tif tokenWidth > idealTokenWidth {\n719\t\t\texcess := tokenWidth - idealTokenWidth\n720\t\t\ttokenWidth = idealTokenWidth\n721\t\t\ttmuxWidth += excess\n722\t\t}\n723\t\n724\t\t// Final safety: ensure widths are positive\n725\t\tif tokenWidth < 1 {\n726\t\t\ttokenWidth = 1\n727\t\t}\n728\t\tif tmuxWidth < 1 {\n729\t\t\ttmuxWidth = 1\n730\t\t}\n731\t\n732\t\tsystemPanel := d.renderSystemPanel(systemWidth, panelHeight)\n733\t\ttokenPanel := d.renderTokenPanel(tokenWidth, panelHeight)\n734\t\ttmuxPanel := d.renderTmuxPanel(tmuxWidth, panelHeight)\n735\t\n736\t\t// Force all panels to exactly the same height using lipgloss\n737\t\t// This ensures borders align even if content varies\n738\t\tuniformHeight := lipgloss.NewStyle().Height(panelHeight)\n739\t\tsystemPanel = uniformHeight.Render(systemPanel)\n740\t\ttokenPanel = uniformHeight.Render(tokenPanel)\n741\t\ttmuxPanel = uniformHeight.Render(tmuxPanel)\n742\t\n743\t\t// Join horizontally with top alignment\n744\t\treturn lipgloss.JoinHorizontal(lipgloss.Top,\n745\t\t\tsystemPanel,\n746\t\t\ttokenPanel,\n747\t\t\ttmuxPanel,\n748\t\t)\n749\t}\n750\t\n751\t// renderWide renders 2 panels on top, 1 on bottom\n752\tfunc (d *Dashboard) renderWide() string {\n753\t\tpanelWidth := (d.width - 3) / 2 // 2 panels with spacing\n754\t\ttopHeight := (d.height - 4) / 2 // Split height\n755\t\tbottomHeight := d.height - topHeight - 4\n756\t\n757\t\tsystemPanel := d.renderSystemPanel(panelWidth, topHeight)\n758\t\ttokenPanel := d.renderTokenPanel(panelWidth, topHeight)\n759\t\ttmuxPanel := d.renderTmuxPanel(d.width-2, bottomHeight)\n760\t\n761\t\ttopRow := lipgloss.JoinHorizontal(lipgloss.Top, systemPanel, \" \", tokenPanel)\n762\t\n763\t\treturn lipgloss.JoinVertical(lipgloss.Left, topRow, tmuxPanel)\n764\t}\n765\t\n766\t// renderNarrow renders panels stacked vertically\n767\tfunc (d *Dashboard) renderNarrow() string {\n768\t\tpanelWidth := d.width - 2\n769\t\tpanelHeight := (d.height - 5) / 3 // 3 panels stacked\n770\t\n771\t\tsystemPanel := d.renderSystemPanel(panelWidth, panelHeight)\n772\t\ttokenPanel := d.renderTokenPanel(panelWidth, panelHeight)\n773\t\ttmuxPanel := d.renderTmuxPanel(panelWidth, panelHeight)\n774\t\n775\t\treturn lipgloss.JoinVertical(lipgloss.Left,\n776\t\t\tsystemPanel,\n777\t\t\ttokenPanel,\n778\t\t\ttmuxPanel,\n779\t\t)\n780\t}\n781\t\n782\t// renderCompact renders panels stacked vertically for narrow terminals (e.g. 75x68):\n783\t// tmux sessions on top, token usage in the middle, system resources on the bottom.\n784\t// Height is distributed with tmux getting extra rows since session lists are tall.\n785\tfunc (d *Dashboard) renderCompact() string {\n786\t\tpanelWidth := d.width - 2\n787\t\tavailable := d.height - 8 // 3×2 border rows + 1 status line + 1 repo/updater line\n788\t\n789\t\t// Give tmux a bit more room — sessions need more lines than the other panels\n790\t\ttmuxHeight := available / 2\n791\t\tremaining := available - tmuxHeight\n792\t\ttokenHeight := remaining / 2\n793\t\tsystemHeight := remaining - tokenHeight\n794\t\n795\t\t// Enforce a sensible minimum so panels don't collapse\n796\t\tif tmuxHeight < 8 {\n797\t\t\ttmuxHeight = 8\n798\t\t}\n799\t\tif tokenHeight < 8 {\n800\t\t\ttokenHeight = 8\n801\t\t}\n802\t\tif systemHeight < 8 {\n803\t\t\tsystemHeight = 8\n804\t\t}\n805\t\n806\t\ttmuxPanel := d.renderTmuxPanel(panelWidth, tmuxHeight)\n807\t\ttokenPanel := d.renderTokenPanel(panelWidth, tokenHeight)\n808\t\tsystemPanel := d.renderSystemPanel(panelWidth, systemHeight)\n809\t\n810\t\treturn lipgloss.JoinVertical(lipgloss.Left,\n811\t\t\ttmuxPanel,\n812\t\t\ttokenPanel,\n813\t\t\tsystemPanel,\n814\t\t)\n815\t}\n816\t\n817\t// renderSystemPanel renders the system resources panel\n818\tfunc (d *Dashboard) renderSystemPanel(width, height int) string {\n819\t\tstyle := panelStyle\n820\t\n821\t\tvar lines []string\n822\t\n823\t\t// Title (with emoji like unified-dashboard)\n824\t\tlines = append(lines, successStyle.Render(\"⚡ System Resources\"))\n825\t\n826\t\t// Load average\n827\t\tif d.systemMetrics.Load.Error == nil {\n828\t\t\tlines = append(lines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Load: %.2f %.2f %.2f\",\n829\t\t\t\td.systemMetrics.Load.Load1,\n830\t\t\t\td.systemMetrics.Load.Load5,\n831\t\t\t\td.systemMetrics.Load.Load15))\n832\t\t} else {\n833\t\t\tlines = append(lines, errorStyle.Render(\"Load: N/A\"))\n834\t\t}\n835\t\n836\t\t// Calculate content width (panel width minus borders and padding)\n837\t\tcontentWidth := width - 4 // -2 for borders, -2 for padding\n838\t\n839\t\t// CPU Total - use same calculation method as Mem/Swap for consistent bar width\n840\t\tif d.systemMetrics.CPU.Error == nil {\n841\t\t\t// Format: \"CPU [|||||| XX.X%]\" - \"CPU \" is 4 chars\n842\t\t\tcpuBarWidth := contentWidth - 4 // Subtract \"CPU \" prefix\n843\t\t\tif cpuBarWidth < 10 {\n844\t\t\t\tcpuBarWidth = 10\n845\t\t\t}\n846\t\t\tlines = append(lines, fmt.Sprintf(\"CPU %s\", d.renderBar(d.systemMetrics.CPU.TotalPercent, cpuBarWidth)))\n847\t\n848\t\t\t// CPU per-core - use up to 6 lines for CPU display\n849\t\t\tmaxCoreLines := 6\n850\t\t\ttotalCores := len(d.systemMetrics.CPU.PerCore)\n851\t\n852\t\t\t// Determine label width based on total cores (for alignment)\n853\t\t\tlabelWidth := 1\n854\t\t\tif totalCores >= 100 {\n855\t\t\t\tlabelWidth = 3\n856\t\t\t} else if totalCores >= 10 {\n857\t\t\t\tlabelWidth = 2\n858\t\t\t}\n859\t\n860\t\t\t// Determine cores per line\n861\t\t\tvar coresPerLine int\n862\t\t\tif totalCores <= 6 {\n863\t\t\t\tcoresPerLine = 1 // One core per line - bars stretch full width\n864\t\t\t} else {\n865\t\t\t\t// Multiple cores per line - calculate how many fit\n866\t\t\t\t// Each core needs: labelWidth + \":[\" + barContent + \"]\" + space\n867\t\t\t\t// Minimum reasonable bar content is about 12 chars\n868\t\t\t\tminCharsPerCore := labelWidth + 3 + 12 // label + \":[]\" + min bar\n869\t\t\t\tcoresPerLine = contentWidth / minCharsPerCore\n870\t\t\t\tif coresPerLine < 2 {\n871\t\t\t\t\tcoresPerLine = 2 // At least 2 per line when splitting\n872\t\t\t\t}\n873\t\t\t}\n874\t\n875\t\t\t// Calculate bar width for cores - align brackets by using fixed widths\n876\t\t\tvar barWidth int\n877\t\t\tif coresPerLine == 1 {\n878\t\t\t\t// Single core per line - match memory/swap calculation for consistency\n879\t\t\t\t// Format: \"NN:[||||... XXX%]\"\n880\t\t\t\t// labelWidth + \":[]\" = labelWidth + 3 chars overhead\n881\t\t\t\tbarWidth = contentWidth - labelWidth - 3\n882\t\t\t\tif barWidth < 10 {\n883\t\t\t\t\tbarWidth = 10\n884\t\t\t\t}\n885\t\t\t} else {\n886\t\t\t\t// Multiple cores per line - split width evenly\n887\t\t\t\t// Account for spaces between cores (1 space separator)\n888\t\t\t\tspacesBetween := coresPerLine - 1\n889\t\t\t\twidthPerCore := (contentWidth - spacesBetween) / coresPerLine\n890\t\t\t\t// Subtract label overhead: labelWidth + \":[]\"\n891\t\t\t\tbarWidth = widthPerCore - labelWidth - 3\n892\t\t\t\tif barWidth < 8 {\n893\t\t\t\t\tbarWidth = 8\n894\t\t\t\t}\n895\t\t\t}\n896\t\n897\t\t\t// Max cores we can display with 6 lines\n898\t\t\tmaxDisplayCores := coresPerLine * maxCoreLines\n899\t\t\tmaxCores := totalCores\n900\t\t\tif maxCores > maxDisplayCores {\n901\t\t\t\tmaxCores = maxDisplayCores\n902\t\t\t}\n903\t\n904\t\t\tvar coreLine strings.Builder\n905\t\t\tlinesUsed := 0\n906\t\t\tfor i := 0; i < maxCores; i++ {\n907\t\t\t\tif i > 0 && i%coresPerLine == 0 {\n908\t\t\t\t\t// Start new line\n909\t\t\t\t\tlines = append(lines, coreLine.String())\n910\t\t\t\t\tcoreLine.Reset()\n911\t\t\t\t\tlinesUsed++\n912\t\t\t\t\tif linesUsed >= maxCoreLines {\n913\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n914\t\t\t\t\t}\n915\t\t\t\t}\n916\t\t\t\tif coreLine.Len() > 0 {\n917\t\t\t\t\tcoreLine.WriteString(\" \")\n918\t\t\t\t}\n919\t\t\t\t// Render progress bar for this core with calculated width\n920\t\t\t\t// Use consistent label width for alignment - brackets align because\n921\t\t\t\t// we use fixed-width labels and fixed-width bar content\n922\t\t\t\tpercent := d.systemMetrics.CPU.PerCore[i]\n923\t\t\t\tminiBar := d.renderMiniBar(percent, barWidth)\n924\t\t\t\tcoreLine.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%*d:[%s]\", labelWidth, i, miniBar))\n925\t\t\t}\n926\t\t\t// Add remaining cores on current line\n927\t\t\tif coreLine.Len() > 0 {\n928\t\t\t\tlines = append(lines, coreLine.String())\n929\t\t\t}\n930\t\n931\t\t\tif totalCores > maxCores {\n932\t\t\t\tlines = append(lines, dimStyle.Render(fmt.Sprintf(\"+%d more cores\", totalCores-maxCores)))\n933\t\t\t}\n934\t\t} else {\n935\t\t\tlines = append(lines, errorStyle.Render(\"CPU: N/A\"))\n936\t\t}\n937\t\n938\t\t// Memory - always compact (one line)\n939\t\tif d.systemMetrics.Memory.Error == nil {\n940\t\t\tmemUsed := metrics.FormatBytes(d.systemMetrics.Memory.Used)\n941\t\t\tmemTotal := metrics.FormatBytes(d.systemMetrics.Memory.Total)\n942\t\t\t// Format: \"Mem [||||...] XX.XX GB/XX.XX GB\"\n943\t\t\t// Calculate bar width: contentWidth - \"Mem \" (4) - \" \" (1) - \"used/total\" - margins\n944\t\t\tbarWidth := contentWidth - 5 - len(memUsed) - 1 - len(memTotal)\n945\t\t\tif barWidth < 10 {\n946\t\t\t\tbarWidth = 10\n947\t\t\t}\n948\t\t\tlines = append(lines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Mem %s %s/%s\",\n949\t\t\t\td.renderBar(d.systemMetrics.Memory.Percentage, barWidth),\n950\t\t\t\tmemUsed, memTotal))\n951\t\t} else {\n952\t\t\tlines = append(lines, errorStyle.Render(\"Mem: N/A\"))\n953\t\t}\n954\t\n955\t\t// Swap - always compact (one line)\n956\t\tif d.systemMetrics.Swap.Error == nil && d.systemMetrics.Swap.Total > 0 {\n957\t\t\tswpUsed := metrics.FormatBytes(d.systemMetrics.Swap.Used)\n958\t\t\tswpTotal := metrics.FormatBytes(d.systemMetrics.Swap.Total)\n959\t\t\t// Use same calculation as Memory for consistency\n960\t\t\tbarWidth := contentWidth - 5 - len(swpUsed) - 1 - len(swpTotal)\n961\t\t\tif barWidth < 10 {\n962\t\t\t\tbarWidth = 10\n963\t\t\t}\n964\t\t\tlines = append(lines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Swp %s %s/%s\",\n965\t\t\t\td.renderBar(d.systemMetrics.Swap.Percentage, barWidth),\n966\t\t\t\tswpUsed, swpTotal))\n967\t\t}\n968\t\n969\t\t// Disk Usage - always compact (one line)\n970\t\tif d.systemMetrics.DiskUsage.Error == nil {\n971\t\t\tdiskUsed := metrics.FormatBytes(d.systemMetrics.DiskUsage.Used)\n972\t\t\tdiskTotal := metrics.FormatBytes(d.systemMetrics.DiskUsage.Total)\n973\t\t\t// Use same calculation as Memory for consistency\n974\t\t\tbarWidth := contentWidth - 5 - len(diskUsed) - 1 - len(diskTotal)\n975\t\t\tif barWidth < 10 {\n976\t\t\t\tbarWidth = 10\n977\t\t\t}\n978\t\t\tlines = append(lines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Dsk %s %s/%s\",\n979\t\t\t\td.renderBar(d.systemMetrics.DiskUsage.Percentage, barWidth),\n980\t\t\t\tdiskUsed, diskTotal))\n981\t\t} else {\n982\t\t\tlines = append(lines, errorStyle.Render(\"Dsk: N/A\"))\n983\t\t}\n984\t\n985\t\t// Disk I/O - verbose format with pipe separators\n986\t\tif d.systemMetrics.DiskIO.Error == nil {\n987\t\t\tlines = append(lines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Disk I/O | Read: %s | Write: %s\",\n988\t\t\t\tmetrics.FormatRate(d.systemMetrics.DiskIO.ReadBytesPerSec),\n989\t\t\t\tmetrics.FormatRate(d.systemMetrics.DiskIO.WriteBytesPerSec)))\n990\t\t} else {\n991\t\t\tlines = append(lines, errorStyle.Render(\"Disk I/O | N/A\"))\n992\t\t}\n993\t\n994\t\t// Net I/O - verbose format with pipe separators\n995\t\tif d.systemMetrics.NetIO.Error == nil {\n996\t\t\tlines = append(lines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Net I/O  | Recv: %s | Sent: %s\",\n997\t\t\t\tmetrics.FormatRate(d.systemMetrics.NetIO.RecvBytesPerSec),\n998\t\t\t\tmetrics.FormatRate(d.systemMetrics.NetIO.SentBytesPerSec)))\n999\t\t} else {\n1000\t\t\tlines = append(lines, errorStyle.Render(\"Net I/O  | N/A\"))\n1001\t\t}\n1002\t\n1003\t\tcontent := strings.Join(lines, \"\\n\")\n1004\t\treturn style.Width(width).Height(height).Render(content)\n1005\t}\n1006\t\n1007\t// renderTokenPanel renders the token usage panel with side-by-side layout\n1008\t// Left side: Total token stats, Right side: Per-model costs\n1009\tfunc (d *Dashboard) renderTokenPanel(width, height int) string {\n1010\t\tstyle := panelStyle\n1011\t\n1012\t\tif d.tokenMetrics == nil {\n1013\t\t\treturn style.Width(width).Height(height).Render(\"Loading token metrics...\")\n1014\t\t}\n1015\t\n1016\t\tcontentWidth := width - 4 // Account for borders and padding\n1017\t\n1018\t\t// Title with lookback info aligned right\n1019\t\ttitle := successStyle.Render(\"💰 Token Usage\")\n1020\t\tlookbackInfo := \"\"\n1021\t\tif d.tokenMetrics != nil && !d.tokenMetrics.LookbackFrom.IsZero() {\n1022\t\t\t// Format start time - use date if not this week\n1023\t\t\tnow := time.Now()\n1024\t\t\tstartTime := d.tokenMetrics.LookbackFrom\n1025\t\t\telapsed := now.Sub(startTime)\n1026\t\n1027\t\t\t// Choose format based on how long ago\n1028\t\t\tvar timeStr string\n1029\t\t\tif elapsed < 7*24*time.Hour {\n1030\t\t\t\ttimeStr = startTime.Format(\"Mon 3:04pm\")\n1031\t\t\t} else {\n1032\t\t\t\ttimeStr = startTime.Format(\"Jan 2 3:04pm\")\n1033\t\t\t}\n1034\t\n1035\t\t\t// Add human-readable duration\n1036\t\t\tdurationStr := metrics.FormatDuration(elapsed)\n1037\t\t\tlookbackInfo = dimStyle.Render(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s → Now (%s)\", timeStr, durationStr))\n1038\t\t} else if d.tokenMetrics != nil {\n1039\t\t\tlookbackInfo = dimStyle.Render(\"All time\")\n1040\t\t}\n1041\t\n1042\t\ttitleLen := lipgloss.Width(title)\n1043\t\tlookbackLen := lipgloss.Width(lookbackInfo)\n1044\t\tspacing := contentWidth - titleLen - lookbackLen\n1045\t\tif spacing < 1 {\n1046\t\t\tspacing = 1\n1047\t\t}\n1048\t\theaderLine := title + strings.Repeat(\" \", spacing) + lookbackInfo\n1049\t\n1050\t\tif !d.tokenMetrics.Available {\n1051\t\t\tvar lines []string\n1052\t\t\tlines = append(lines, headerLine)\n1053\t\t\tlines = append(lines, errorStyle.Render(\"Not Available\"))\n1054\t\t\tif d.tokenMetrics.Error != \"\" {\n1055\t\t\t\tlines = append(lines, wrapText(d.tokenMetrics.Error, width-4))\n1056\t\t\t}\n1057\t\t\tcontent := strings.Join(lines, \"\\n\")\n1058\t\t\treturn style.Width(width).Height(height).Render(content)\n1059\t\t}\n1060\t\n1061\t\t// Helper to get model style by name\n1062\t\tgetModelStyle := func(modelName string) lipgloss.Style {\n1063\t\t\tif strings.Contains(modelName, \"opus\") {\n1064\t\t\t\treturn lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color(\"#ff6b6b\")) // Red for Opus\n1065\t\t\t} else if strings.Contains(modelName, \"sonnet\") {\n1066\t\t\t\treturn lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color(\"#4ecdc4\")) // Cyan for Sonnet\n1067\t\t\t} else if strings.Contains(modelName, \"haiku\") {\n1068\t\t\t\treturn lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color(\"#95e1d3\")) // Light green for Haiku\n1069\t\t\t} else if strings.Contains(modelName, \"glm\") {\n1070\t\t\t\treturn lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color(\"#00bfff\")) // Blue for GLM\n1071\t\t\t}\n1072\t\t\treturn dimStyle\n1073\t\t}\n1074\t\n1075\t\t// Build left column: Total stats\n1076\t\tvar leftLines []string\n1077\t\thasCacheRead := d.tokenMetrics.CacheReadTokens > 0\n1078\t\thasCacheCreate := d.tokenMetrics.CacheCreationTokens > 0\n1079\t\thasRate := d.tokenMetrics.Rate > 0\n1080\t\thasAvg := d.tokenMetrics.SessionAvgRate > 0\n1081\t\n1082\t\t// Compact format for left column\n1083\t\tleftLines = append(leftLines, fmt.Sprintf(\"In:    %s\", metrics.FormatTokensCompact(d.tokenMetrics.InputTokens)))\n1084\t\tleftLines = append(leftLines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Out:   %s\", metrics.FormatTokensCompact(d.tokenMetrics.OutputTokens)))\n1085\t\tif hasCacheRead {\n1086\t\t\tleftLines = append(leftLines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Cache: %s\", metrics.FormatTokensCompact(d.tokenMetrics.CacheReadTokens)))\n1087\t\t}\n1088\t\tif hasCacheCreate {\n1089\t\t\tleftLines = append(leftLines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Create:%s\", metrics.FormatTokensCompact(d.tokenMetrics.CacheCreationTokens)))\n1090\t\t}\n1091\t\tleftLines = append(leftLines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Total: %s\", boldStyle.Render(metrics.FormatTokensCompact(d.tokenMetrics.TotalTokens))))\n1092\t\tleftLines = append(leftLines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Reqs:  %d\", d.tokenMetrics.Prompts))\n1093\t\tleftLines = append(leftLines, fmt.Sprintf(\"Cost:  %s\", costStyle.Render(metrics.FormatCost(d.tokenMetrics.TotalCost))))\n1094\t\tif hasRate {\n1095\t\t\tleftLines = a progress bar with percentage inside (unified-dashboard style)\n1904\tfunc (d *Dashboard) renderBar(percent float64, width int) string {\n1905\t\tif width < 10 {\n1906\t\t\treturn \"\"\n1907\t\t}\n1908\t\n1909\t\t// Determine color based on threshold (unified-dashboard style)\n1910\t\tvar color string\n1911\t\tif percent >= 95 {\n1912\t\t\tcolor = \"#ff0000\" // Red\n1913\t\t} else if percent >= 80 {\n1914\t\t\tcolor = \"#ffaa00\" // Orange\n1915\t\t} else if percent >= 60 {\n1916\t\t\tcolor = \"#ffff00\" // Yellow\n1917\t\t} else {\n1918\t\t\tcolor = \"#00ff00\" // Green\n1919\t\t}\n1920\t\n1921\t\t// Format percentage\n1922\t\tpercentText := fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f%%\", percent)\n1923\t\n1924\t\t// Calculate fill width (accounting for percentage text)\n1925\t\tbarWidth := width - 2 // Account for brackets\n1926\t\tavailableWidth := barWidth - len(percentText) - 1 // -1 for space before %\n1927\t\tfillWidth := int(percent / 100.0 * float64(availableWidth))\n1928\t\tif fillWidth > availableWidth {\n1929\t\t\tfillWidth = availableWidth\n1930\t\t}\n1931\t\tif fillWidth < 0 {\n1932\t\t\tfillWidth = 0\n1933\t\t}\n1934\t\n1935\t\t// availableWidth-fillWidth)\n1938\t\n1939\t\t// Apply styling\n1940\t\tbarStyle := lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color(color))\n1941\t\tdimStyle := lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color(\"#888888\"))\n1942\t\n1943\t\tvar bar strings.Builder\n1944\t\tbar.WriteString(\"[\")\n1945\t\tbar.WriteString(barStyle.Render(filled))\n1946\t\tbar.WriteString(dimStyle.Render(empty))\n1947\t\tbar.WriteString(\" \")\n1948\t\tbar.WriteString(percentText)\n1949\t\tbar.WriteString(\"]\")\n1950\t\n1951\t\treturn bar.String()\n1952\t}\n1953\t\n1954\t// renderMiniBar creates a compact progress bar with percentage inside\n1955\t// Format: \"||| 42%\" for use in CPU core display\n1956\t// Returns a fixed-width string to ensure bracket alignment\n1957\tfunc (d *Dashboard) renderMiniBar(percent float64, barWidth int) string {\n1958\t\t// Determine color based on threshold\n1959\t\tvar color string\n1960\t\tif percent >= 95 {\n1961\t\t\tcolor = \"#ff0000\" // Red\n1962\t\t} else if percent >= 80 {\n1963\t\t\tcolor = \"#ffaa00\" // Orange\n1964\t\t} else if percent >= 60 {\n1965\t\t\tcolor = \"#ffff00\" // Yellow\n1966\t\t} else {\n1967\t\t\tcolor = \"#00ff00\" // Green\n1968\t\t}\n1969\t\n1970\t\t// Format percentage with fixed width (4 chars: \"XXX%\" or \" XX%\")\n1971\t\tpercentText := fmt.Sprintf(\"%3.0f%%\", percent)\n1972\t\n1973\t\t// Reserve space for percentage text (4 chars) + 1 space\n1974\t\tpercentSpace := 5\n1975\t\tbarAvailableWidth := barWidth - percentSpace\n1976\t\tif barAvailableWidth < 1 {\n1977\t\t\tbarAvailableWidth = 1\n1978\t\t}\n1979\t\n1980\t\t// Calculate fill width\n1981\t\tfillWidth := int(percent / 100.0 * float64(barAvailableWidth))\n1982\t\tif fillWidth > barAvailableWidth {\n1983\t\t\tfillWidth = barAvailableWidth\n1984\t\t}\n1985\t\tif fillWidth < 0 {\n1986\t\t\tfillWidth = 0\n1987\t\t}\n1988\t\n1989\t\t// Create filled and empty portions\n1990\t\tfilled := strings.Repeat(\"|\", lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color(color))\n1995\t\tdimStyle := lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color(\"#888888\"))\n1996\t\n1997\t\treturn barStyle.Render(filled) + dimStyle.Render(empty) + \" \" + percentText\n1998\t}\n1999\t\n2000\t// Styles (unified-dashboard palette)\n2001\tvar (\n2002\t\tpanelStyle = others read from cache\nfunc (d *Dashboard) collectMetrics() tea.Cmd {\n\treturn func() tea.Msg {\n\t\tcache := d.tokenCollector.GetCache()\n\t\tisLeader :=
